9 Prep Data File for Paragon

panel_snps <- readRDS(here("data","derived","panel_snps"))

Prep a BED file

Bed file basics are chrom, chromStart, and chromEnd.

In this case, starting with chrom and position

Adjust so chromStart is the position and chromEnd is chromStart + 1 and so instead of “1” it is “chr1”

bed <- panel_snps %>%
  mutate(chromEnd = pos +1) %>%
  rename(chromStart = pos) %>%
  mutate(holder = "chr") %>%
  mutate(chrom = paste(holder,chrom,sep="")) %>%
  select(chrom,chromStart,chromEnd)
as_tibble(bed)

write.table(bed, file = here("data","derived","panel_snps.bed"),quote = FALSE, sep = "\t", col.names = FALSE, row.names = FALSE)
